ex11. Causal (Same backend, CRP Backend) - Cauchy/Laplace

Website workflow note. This page reflects the current exported API and recommended wrapper-first usage. Last updated: 2026-02-19.

For the full package narrative, see the main package vignettes (basic, unconditional, conditional, and causal).

Causal Inference: Mixed Backends (CRP+SB)

This vignette fits two causal models using different backends and kernels:

  • Model A: CRP bulk-only (Cauchy)
  • Model B: SB with GPD tail (Laplace)

Each model demonstrates the full causal S3 workflow: bundle, fit, predict, plot, ATE, and QTE.

What you’ll learn

  • How backend choice (CRP vs SB) and tail choice (GPD = FALSE/TRUE) affect predictive uncertainty and downstream causal estimands.

  • How to keep comparisons interpretable by using the same post-fit S3 surface across models (summary(), predict(), plot()).

  • How to read both mean and quantile effect summaries and treat them as model-based functionals. ## When to use this template

  • You want an apples-to-apples comparison of causal models that differ by backend and/or tail augmentation.

  • You want a compact example of the full causal S3 workflow in one place. ## Next steps

  • Use the “same-backend” causal examples to isolate tail effects from backend effects.

Data Setup

Code 
data("causal_alt_real500_p4_k2")
y <- causal_alt_real500_p4_k2$y
A <- causal_alt_real500_p4_k2$A
X <- as.matrix(causal_alt_real500_p4_k2$X)

summary_tbl <- tibble(
  statistic = c("N", "Mean", "SD", "Min", "Max"),
  value = c(length(y), mean(y), sd(y), min(y), max(y))
)

summary_tbl
# A tibble: 5 × 2
  statistic   value
  <chr>       <dbl>
1 N         500    
2 Mean        0.274
3 SD          1.76 
4 Min        -8.09 
5 Max         5.27
Code 
x_eval <- X[1:40, , drop = FALSE]
y_eval <- y[1:40]
u_threshold <- as.numeric(stats::quantile(y, 0.8, names = FALSE))
Code 
df_causal <- data.frame(y = y, A = as.factor(A), x1 = X[, 1], x2 = X[, 2])

p_scatter <- ggplot(df_causal, aes(x = x1, y = y, color = A)) +
  geom_point(alpha = 0.5) +
  labs(title = "Outcome vs X1 by Treatment", x = "X1", y = "y", color = "Treatment") +
  theme_minimal()

p_scatter

Model A: CRP Bulk-only (Cauchy)

Code 
bundle_crp_bulk <- bundle(
  x = y,
  treat = A,
  X = X,
  kernel = "cauchy",
  backend = "crp",
  PS = "logit",
  GPD = FALSE,
  components = 5,
  mcmc_outcome = list(niter = 2500, nburnin = 500, nchains = 1, thin = 1, seed = 1),
  mcmc_ps = list(niter = 2500, nburnin = 500, nchains = 1, thin = 1, seed = 1)
)

bundle_crp_bulk
CausalMixGPD causal bundle
PS model: Bayesian logit (A | X)

Code 
fit_crp_bulk <- quiet_mcmc(dpmix.causal(bundle_crp_bulk))
summary(fit_crp_bulk)

Model B: SB with GPD Tail (Laplace)

Code 
param_specs_gpd <- list(
  gpd = list(
    threshold = list(
      mode = "dist",
      dist = "lognormal",
      args = list(meanlog = log(max(u_threshold, .Machine$double.eps)), sdlog = 0.25)
    )
  )
)

bundle_sb_gpd <- bundle(
  x = y,
  treat = A,
  X = X,
  kernel = "laplace",
  backend = "sb",
  PS = "logit",
  GPD = TRUE,
  components = 5,
  param_specs = param_specs_gpd,
  mcmc_outcome = list(niter = 2500, nburnin = 500, nchains = 1, thin = 1, seed = 2),
  mcmc_ps = list(niter = 2500, nburnin = 500, nchains = 1, thin = 1, seed = 2)
)
